    (function() {
     (function() {
       var height, i, images, width;
       if (window.location.pathname === '/casinos' || window.location.pathname === '/casinos/new' || window.location.pathname === '/casinos/mobile') {
         images = document.getElementsByTagName('img');
         i = 0;
         while (i < images.length) {
           width = images[i].clientWidth > 0 ? images[i].clientWidth : 0;
           height = images[i].clientHeight > 0 ? images[i].clientHeight : 0;
           if (width !== 0) {
             images[i].setAttribute('width', width);
           }
           if (height !== 0) {
             images[i].setAttribute('height', height);
           }
           i++;
         }
       }
     })();
   
   }).call(this);
   </script>

   <script>
    (function() {
     $(function() {
       $(document).trigger('filter:before');
       $('[data-filter_autosubmit=1]').bind({
         change: function(e) {
           var form_id, form_object;
           form_id = $(e.target).attr('form');
           form_object = $("#" + form_id);
           $("input[form=" + form_id + "]").clone().css('visibility', 'hidden').appendTo(form_object).attr("class", "filtersCloned");
           $('select[form=' + form_id + ']').each(function() {
             return $('<input/>').attr('type', 'hidden').attr('name', $(this).attr('name')).val($(this).val()).appendTo(form_object).attr("class", "filtersCloned");
           });
           if (form_object.data('commit_in_progress') != null) {
             return;
           }
           form_object.bind('ajax:complete', function() {
             $(this).removeData('commit_in_progress');
             return $(".filtersCloned").remove();
           });
           return form_object.data('commit_in_progress', 1).submit();
         }
       });
       new FiltersForm({
         form_selector: '#filters_form',
         more_button_selector: '#more_button',
         overall_count_selector: '#overall_count'
       });
       return $("#filters_search_input").unbind('keydown').bind({
         keydown: function(e) {
           var keycode;
           keycode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which;
           if (keycode === 13) {
             return $(this).trigger("change");
           }
         }
       });
     });
   
   }).call(this);
   </script>

    (function() {
     $(function() {
       var cookie, cookies, key;
       if (!$.cookie('created_at')) {
         cookies = $.cookie();
         for (key in cookies) {
           cookie = cookies[key];
           $.removeCookie(key, {
             path: '/'
           });
         }
         return $.cookie('created_at', new Date());
       }
     });
   
   }).call(this);
